",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"system_prompt_length"}]," 表示原始长度。"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":["\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"sensitiveSpanAttributeMaxLength"}],"（例如，降至
